It is important to recognise that Galton did not design these methods for purely scientific purposes. He used them to obsessively rank just about any aspect of human life. Among other things, for instance, he was the first man to statistically rank women from different areas in terms of attractiveness. Not only was this determined by his own judgements, it was also done in secret, with a clicker he used in his pocket whenever he saw a woman out in public. This began a misogynistic tradition of numerically ranking women that continues to this day. Facebook, for instance, was first made as a site for ranking the attractiveness of female college students, before it grew into the social media giant it is today.

必须认识到，高尔顿设计这些方法并非纯粹出于科学目的。他痴迷于用这些方法对人类生活的几乎所有方面进行排名。例如，他是第一个根据吸引力对不同地区女性进行统计排名的人。这不仅基于他个人的判断，而且是在秘密中进行的——每当在公共场合看到女性，他都会用口袋里的计数器偷偷记录。这开启了一种用数字给女性排名的厌女传统，并延续至今。例如，Facebook 最初就是一个为女大学生吸引力排名的网站，后来才发展成为今天的社交媒体巨头。



It was also Galton that proved identity could be detected through fingerprinting technology, thus paving the way for scientific control of the criminalised. In this, he helped formalise a technique that would allow the prison industrial complex to grow rapidly. In his laboratory, he recorded both the mental abilities and biometric markers of thousands of Londoners, generating aggregates and analysing individuals in relation to statistical norms to judge their worth. It was his work on mental ability that paved the way for subsequent intelligence tests developed by Alfred Binet and Théodore Simon – and grounded the psychometric and biometric research methods used in the following century.

同样也是高尔顿证明了身份可以通过指纹识别技术来确认，从而为科学管控罪犯铺平了道路。在这一过程中，他帮助规范了一种技术，使得监狱工业复合体得以迅速发展。在他的实验室里，他记录了数千名伦敦人的心智能力和生物特征标记，通过生成汇总数据并对照统计规范分析个体，以评判他们的价值。正是他在心智能力方面的研究，为阿尔弗雷德·比奈和西奥多·西蒙后来开发的智力测试奠定了基础，并确立了随后一个世纪中使用的心理测量和生物测量研究方法。



Just as importantly, with Galton we see not just the development of new methods but also an ideological shift. Despite Quetelet’s influence, Galton eventually came to suggest that the average was, while better than sub-normality, still something to be overcome rather than being the ideal state as Quetelet had envisioned. Essentially Galton was more interested in variation and rank, with the average sitting in the middle of his ranking rather than being seen as a form of perfection in itself. This was primarily based on his interest in genius and idiocy, but also on his fears of racial degeneration, and the idea, in his own words, that those who ‘deviate widely from the mean’ risk the race’s reversion to ‘that mediocrity, whence the majority of their ancestors originally sprang’.10

同样重要的是，在高尔顿这里，我们不仅看到了新方法的发展，还见证了一种意识形态的转变。尽管受到凯特莱的影响，高尔顿最终提出，平均值虽然优于次正常状态，但仍需被超越，而非如凯特莱所设想的那样是理想状态。本质上，高尔顿更关注变异和等级，平均值位于他等级体系的中间位置，而非被视为一种完美的形式。这主要基于他对天才与白痴的兴趣，也源于他对种族退化的恐惧，以及他本人所言：那些“严重偏离平均值”的人，可能会使种族回归到“那种平庸状态，即他们大多数祖先最初所起源的状态”。 10



While it is apparent, in retrospect, that Galton’s misogyny, racism, and class ideology drove much of his thinking, it is notable that he was quite explicit in the significance of productivity in his later ranking systems. ‘Energy’, he wrote in 1883, ‘is the capacity for labour’ and is ‘consistent with all the robust virtues, and makes a large practice of them possible’. In turn, he went on, energy ‘is the measure of fulness of life; the more energy the more abundance of it; no energy at all is death; idiots are feeble and listless’. And of course, he also associated higher productivity with what he took to be racial superiority, positing that energy is ‘an attribute of the higher races, being favoured beyond all other qualities by natural selection’.11 Hence his later work moved away from the more unambiguously value-laden notion of ‘eminence’ and instead sought to associate fitness with productivity in order to ground it in, so he thought, a more objective Darwinian analysis.

回顾过去，高尔顿的性别歧视、种族主义和阶级意识形态显然在很大程度上驱动了他的思想，但值得注意的是，他在后来的排名体系中明确强调了生产力的重要性。他在 1883 年写道：“精力是劳动的能力”，并且“与所有强健的美德相一致，使它们的大规模实践成为可能”。他接着指出，精力“是生命充实程度的衡量标准；精力越多，生命就越丰盈；毫无精力即是死亡；白痴则虚弱无力、无精打采”。当然，他还将更高的生产力与他所认为的种族优越性联系起来，假设精力是“高等种族的属性，在自然选择中比其他所有品质更受青睐”。 11 因此，他后来的研究逐渐远离了更为明确带有价值判断的“卓越”概念，转而试图将适应性与生产力联系起来，以便将其建立在他认为更为客观的达尔文分析基础之上。



Yet as Donald Mackenzie later put it, in Galton and his followers we see ‘the practice and experience of the intellectual aristocracy read onto nature’.12 Mackenzie’s work links this precisely to the class structures in Britain at the time. In his own words:

然而正如唐纳德·麦肯齐后来所言，在高尔顿及其追随者身上，我们看到的是"知识贵族阶层的实践与经验被投射到自然之中"。 12 麦肯齐的研究将这一点精确地联系到当时英国的阶级结构。用他自己的话说：





The core of this view was the idea that social position was (or at least should be) the consequence of individual mental ability. There was a natural hierarchy of talent which could be translated into a social hierarchy of occupations. At the top were the professions, with leading businessmen sometimes admitted into the elite: they represented the pick of the nation’s brains. Below them were useful but increasingly dull-brained groups: small businessmen, clerks, shop-keepers, foremen, skilled workers. These were socially valuable, if not as valuable as the professional. Finally, there came strata who were typically stupid or worse: the unskilled, the unemployed and the outcast.13

这种观念的核心在于：社会地位是（或至少应当是）个人心智能力的产物。天赋存在天然等级，这种等级可以转化为职业的社会等级。处于顶端的是专业人士，有时杰出的商界领袖也能跻身精英阶层：他们代表着国家智慧的精华。其下是有用但头脑日益愚钝的群体：小商人、职员、店主、工头、技术工人。这些人在社会上有其价值，尽管不如专业人士那般重要。最后，则是那些通常愚钝或更糟的阶层：非技术工人、失业者与社会弃儿。 13





In this, according to Mackenzie, the statistical and methodological innovations developed by Galton were not simply objective discoveries. Rather, while they did have scientific utility, they were simultaneously innovations that reflected and in turn helped naturalise the ideology of the time. In turn, their uses in scientific research would help to naturalise the cognitive, economic, gendered, and racial hierarchies of capitalist and imperialist Britain.

麦肯齐指出，高尔顿所发展的统计与方法论创新并非仅仅是客观发现。相反，尽管它们确实具有科学实用性，但同时也是反映并进而帮助固化当时意识形态的创新。相应地，它们在科学研究中的应用将有助于使资本主义和帝国主义英国的认知、经济、性别和种族等级制度显得自然化。



Ultimately, what all this would lead toward would be Galton’s proposal of the new science of ‘eugenics’ in the 1880s. Initially, it was Galton’s concern with surpassing the average that inspired the key theoretical change underlying what he referred to as the ‘method of statistics by intercomparison’.14 This consisted largely in substituting Quetelet’s mean for the median. The disability historian Lennard Davis has emphasised how it was this shift in statistical method that was used to justify Galton’s attempts to rank individuals and populations from the most to least fit. For while ‘high intelligence in a’ Quetelian ‘normal distribution would simply be an extreme’ and thus undesirable, under a Galtonian ‘system it would become the highest ranked trait’.15 As Galton wrote in 1883, the ‘median value may be accepted as the average’ due to representing not the ideal, but rather the ‘multitude of mediocre values’ between the highest and the lowest abilities.16

最终，这一切将导向高尔顿在 19 世纪 80 年代提出的新科学——“优生学”。最初，正是高尔顿对超越平均水平的关注，激发了他所谓“通过相互比较的统计方法”背后的关键理论变革。 14 这主要在于用中位数取代了凯特莱的平均值。残障历史学家伦纳德·戴维斯强调，正是这种统计方法的转变，被用来为高尔顿试图将个人和群体从最适者到最不适者进行排序的做法提供依据。因为在凯特莱的“正态分布中，高智商仅仅是一个极端”，因而并不理想；而在高尔顿的“体系中，它将成为最高等级的特征”。 15 正如高尔顿在 1883 年所写，中位数“可以被接受为平均值”，因为它代表的不是理想值，而是最高能力与最低能力之间“大量平庸的数值”。 16



It was this shift that allowed Galton to present his newly coined concept of eugenics. He defined eugenics as: ‘the science of improving stock […] to give to the more suitable races or strains of blood a better chance of prevailing’.17 Based on his new methods for ranking individuals and groups, Galton argued that the role of governments should be to improve the average range of successive generations. And thus it was precisely with Galton’s work, as Stephens and Cryle have stressed, that ‘the idea of the application of normal as a cultural practice’ finally emerged.18 In other words, Galton formalised, and provided a veneer of scientific legitimacy to, the informal normalising practices we covered in the previous chapter. It was this that would legitimise a mass expansion of these practices over the following decades – and, as we shall come back to, would in time be used to justify some of the worst atrocities ever committed.

正是这一转变使得高尔顿得以提出他新创造的优生学概念。他将优生学定义为："改良血统的科学……使更适宜的种族或血统获得更有利的优胜机会"。 17 基于其新建立的个体与群体分级方法，高尔顿主张政府的职责应是提升连续世代的平均水准。正如斯蒂芬斯和克莱尔所强调的，正是在高尔顿的研究中，"将常态作为文化实践加以应用的理念"最终得以确立。 18 换言之，高尔顿将前一章所述的非正式规范化实践进行了体系化，并为其披上了科学合法性的外衣。正是这一点使得这些实践在随后数十年间大规模扩张获得正当性——正如我们后续将探讨的，这种理念最终被用来为某些史上最恶劣的暴行提供辩护。



KRAEPELIN’S GALTONIANISATION OF PSYCHIATRY

克雷佩林对精神病学的高尔顿式改造



We have just considered how Galton began to develop the idea of the normal mind in such a way that allowed him to rank the mental functioning of individuals and groups from the lowest to highest. This was taken up in a range of sciences. The influence of Galton on psychological and psychometric research has been well established elsewhere. The most notable work on this is Kurt Danziger’s book Constructing the Subject: Historical Origins of Psychological Research, which establishes how Galton’s theories and methods formed the basis for much research since this time. As was noted above, Galton is also widely acknowledged as having provided much of the basis for behavioural genetics. By contrast, his influence has been curiously overlooked in psychiatry, and Galton is barely mentioned in general histories of the discipline.

我们刚刚探讨了高尔顿如何开始发展正常心智的概念，这种方式使他能够将个体和群体的心理功能从最低到最高进行排序。这一理念被一系列科学领域所采纳。高尔顿对心理学和心理测量学研究的影响在其他地方已有充分论述。其中最著名的研究是库尔特·丹齐格的著作《构建主体：心理学研究的历史起源》，该书确立了高尔顿的理论和方法如何成为此后大量研究的基础。如前所述，高尔顿还被广泛认为是行为遗传学基础的主要贡献者。相比之下，他在精神病学领域的影响却被奇怪地忽视了，在该学科的一般历史中，高尔顿几乎未被提及。



Yet Galton’s influence on psychiatry was in fact highly significant. While he inspired a number of doctors, the most notable to expand Galton’s paradigm was the most prominent of all nineteenth-century German psychiatrists, Emil Kraepelin. Today, Kraepelin is widely credited with developing the biocentric, classificatory approach adopted both in the German psychiatry that dominated during his time before being reborn in the DSM from 1980 onward. His legacy is typically associated with his quest to turn psychiatry into a firmly scientific discipline, continuous with general medicine. In large part, he is taken to have done this through adopting a naturalistic and experimental approach, alongside attention to classifications he sought to map on to biological aetiology. Viewed in the context covered here, however, it would be more accurate to say that Kraepelin – who, in his autobiography, recalled Galton as a ‘fine old gentleman, who stimulated the field of psychology’19 – essentially expanded the scope of Galton’s paradigm.

然而，高尔顿对精神病学的影响实际上极为深远。尽管他启发了许多医生，但将高尔顿范式发扬光大的最杰出人物，当属十九世纪德国最著名的精神病学家埃米尔·克雷佩林。如今，克雷佩林被广泛认为是开创了生物中心主义分类法的先驱，这一方法不仅主导了他所处时代的德国精神病学，更在 1980 年后通过《精神疾病诊断与统计手册》（DSM）得以重生。他的遗产通常与将精神病学转变为严谨科学学科的努力联系在一起，使其与普通医学保持连续性。在很大程度上，人们认为他通过采用自然主义和实验性方法，并关注其试图与生物病因学相对应的分类体系，实现了这一目标。然而，从本文所探讨的背景来看，更准确的说法是：克雷佩林——他在自传中回忆高尔顿时称其为“一位杰出的老绅士，推动了心理学领域的发展”——实质上扩展了高尔顿范式的范畴。



Kraepelin himself was born in 1856 in a small town in the north of Germany called Neustrelitz. When Kraepelin began studying psychology and medicine at the University of Leipzig, both psychology and psychiatry had only just begun to emerge in response to the broader economic and historical shifts detailed in the previous chapters. They were not yet proper sciences with anything like a coherent unifying paradigm. In fact, Kraepelin himself had initially been more inspired by his teacher Wilhelm Wundt, whose pioneering experimental psychology focused on individual introspection and not collective aggregates. Yet by the early twentieth century, the Wundtian method had deteriorated while the Galtonian approach was, as Danziger writes, ‘extending its appeal with every passing year’ as ‘it proved itself capable of generating exciting methodological innovations that promised to extend the scope of scientific psychology far beyond what had hitherto been thought possible’.20 And it was in this approach, which was then fast becoming accepted as the correct basis for psychological, psychometric, and biometric research, that Kraepelin envisioned the grounds for a new, scientific psychiatry.

克雷佩林本人于 1856 年出生在德国北部一个名为新施特雷利茨的小镇。当克雷佩林开始在莱比锡大学学习心理学和医学时，心理学和精神病学都才刚刚兴起，这是对前几章详述的更广泛的经济和历史变迁的回应。它们还不是拥有连贯统一范式的真正科学。事实上，克雷佩林最初更多地受到他的老师威廉·冯特的启发，冯特开创性的实验心理学专注于个体内省，而非集体聚合。然而到了二十世纪初，冯特的方法已经衰落，而高尔顿的方法正如丹齐格所写，“其吸引力与日俱增”，因为“它证明了自己能够产生令人兴奋的方法论创新，这些创新有望将科学心理学的范围扩展到迄今为止被认为不可能的程度”。 20 正是在这种方法中，克雷佩林构想了一种新的、科学的精神病学的基础，而这种方法当时正迅速被接受为心理学、心理测量学和生物统计学研究的正确基础。



While much of Kraepelin’s work focused on clinical understanding, we see the Galtonian influence when we consider his more theoretical work. This was stated most clearly in Kraepelin’s 1919 essay ‘Ends and Means of Psychiatric Research’, where he proposed an unmistakably Galtonian vision for the future of what he termed ‘mass psychiatry’. In his own words:

虽然克雷佩林的大部分工作侧重于临床理解，但当我们审视他更具理论性的著作时，便能发现高尔顿的影响。这一点在克雷佩林 1919 年的论文《精神病学研究的目的与手段》中表述得最为清晰，他在文中为所谓的"大众精神病学"的未来提出了一个明确带有高尔顿色彩的愿景。用他自己的话说：





By […] determining the range of normal variation, we shall obtain a standard for measuring morbid deviations – a standard that will be of value, not merely for pure science, but for many practical purposes, as for estimating school capacity, military fitness, business talent, and responsibility […] Thus we may gradually learn, not only to characterise numerically the various grades amid kinds of intellectual defect, but to obtain more exact expressions for insufficiencies and aberrances in other mental spheres. Only thus can the important forms of psychopathy that fade into one another be more clearly outlined.21

通过确定正常变异的范围，我们将获得一个衡量病态偏差的标准——这个标准不仅对纯科学有价值，对许多实际用途也至关重要，例如评估学习能力、军事适应性、商业才能以及责任承担能力。因此，我们或许能逐步学会不仅用数字来表征各类智力缺陷的不同等级，还能为其他心理领域中的不足与偏差获得更精确的表达方式。唯有如此，那些相互交融的重要精神病理形态才能得到更清晰的勾勒。 21





In other words, what Kraepelin envisioned was expanding the approach Galton had developed to study intelligence. It would now encompass every other aspect of the mind, including as a basis for psychiatry but also for a variety of roles in relation to the shifting needs of capital in education, the workplace, and so forth. The hope was that expanding this method would allow a greater and more specific understanding of a wide range of dysfunctions that could then be treated and controlled.

换句话说，克雷佩林所设想的是扩展高尔顿为研究智力而开发的方法。它将涵盖心智的各个方面，不仅作为精神病学的基础，还能满足资本在教育、职场等领域不断变化的需求，发挥多种作用。人们希望，通过扩展这种方法，能够更广泛、更具体地理解各种功能障碍，从而加以治疗和控制。



In turn, for Kraepelin, the ends of psychiatry, and its use of these methods, likewise echoed the Galtonian hope for bio-cultural normalisation and improvement. As Kraepelin put it:

反过来，对克雷佩林而言，精神病学的目标及其对这些方法的应用，同样呼应了高尔顿对生物文化正常化与改善的期望。正如克雷佩林所言：





The psychiatric importance of such investigation on the large scale cannot be over-estimated. A mass psychiatry, having at its disposal statistics in their widest scope, must provide the foundations for a science of public mental health – a preventive psychological medicine for combating all those mischiefs that we group under the head of mental degeneracy.22

大规模此类调查的精神病学重要性再怎么高估也不为过。一种拥有最广泛统计数据的群体精神病学，必须为公共心理健康科学奠定基础——这是一种预防性心理医学，旨在对抗我们归类为精神退化的一切危害。 22





Part of the worry here, Kraepelin went on, was that ‘an ever-widening stream of inferior stock [is mixing] itself with our offspring, [contributing] to the deterioration of the race’.23 Thus, for Kraepelin as for Galton, the concept of the normal mind was utilised precisely because it grounded the broader political project of biological and cultural control.

克拉佩林进一步指出，这种担忧的部分原因在于，"劣等血统的洪流正日益扩大，与我们的后代相混合，导致种族退化"。 23 因此，对克拉佩林而言，正如对高尔顿一样，正常心智这一概念之所以被采用，正是因为它为更广泛的生物与文化控制政治计划奠定了基础。



It was through this underlying framework that Kraepelin began the still ongoing project of dividing up mental disorders into different kinds and levels of subnormal functioning, with a focus on heredity, severity, development, and outcome throughout the lifespan. And in turn this approach was adopted in German psychiatry – which was very much a world leader in the psychiatry of the time – thus allowing a growing number of new classifications to be specified, studied, and controlled.

正是基于这一根本框架，克拉佩林开启了至今仍在持续的精神障碍分类工程，将其划分为不同类型和程度的功能低下，并重点关注遗传性、严重程度、发展过程以及整个生命周期的结果。随后，这一方法被德国精神病学所采纳——当时的德国精神病学无疑是世界领先的——从而使得越来越多的新分类得以被界定、研究和控制。



Indeed, eugenic thinking became so popular among psychiatrists that it was even included in influential textbooks of the time. Most notable here was the psychiatrist Eugene Bleuler, known for coining the terms ‘schizophrenia’ and ‘autism’. In his 1924 Textbook of Psychiatry, Bleuler openly stated his view that the ‘more severely burdened should not propagate themselves’ in case the race would ‘rapidly deteriorate’.24 Thus Kraepelin and his contemporaries expanded the Galtonian paradigm to form the basis for modern psychiatry, while the same metaphysics came to underpin the emerging fields of clinical, abnormal, and developmental psychology.

事实上，优生学思想在精神病学家中变得如此流行，甚至被纳入了当时颇具影响力的教科书中。其中最值得注意的是精神病学家尤金·布洛伊勒，他以创造了"精神分裂症"和"孤独谱系"这两个术语而闻名。在他 1924 年的《精神病学教科书》中，布洛伊勒公开表达了他的观点，即"负担更重的人不应繁衍后代"，以免种族"迅速退化"。 24 因此，克雷佩林及其同时代人扩展了高尔顿的范式，为现代精神病学奠定了基础，而同样的形而上学思想也开始支撑着临床心理学、变态心理学和发展心理学这些新兴领域。



---

Empire of Normality



4



The eugenics movement

优生学运动



We first see the political and cultural effects of Galton’s eugenic ideology in Britain. Inspired by Galton, the Eugenic Education Society was founded in 1906 (renamed as the Eugenics Society in 1924 and then as the Galton Institute in 1989).1 In the early days the society included prominent members such as the economist John Maynard Keynes, the biologist Julian Huxley, and Galton himself. Among many other proposals, the society endorsed involuntary euthanasia of the ‘feeble-minded’ alongside funds for the wealthy to reproduce in higher numbers. While the British government rejected the Eugenic Education Society’s proposals for compulsory sterilisation of the feeble-minded, it did vote in the 1913 Mental Deficiency Act to begin mass segregation based on proximity to cognitive normality. Winston Churchill himself stated in the Act’s support that the ‘unnatural and increasingly rapid growth of the feeble-minded classes, coupled with a steady restriction among the thrifty, energetic and superior stocks constitutes a race danger’.2

我们首先在英国看到了高尔顿优生学思想的政治和文化影响。受高尔顿启发，优生教育学会于 1906 年成立（1924 年更名为优生学会，1989 年更名为高尔顿研究所）。 1 该学会早期成员包括经济学家约翰·梅纳德·凯恩斯、生物学家朱利安·赫胥黎以及高尔顿本人等杰出人物。在众多提议中，该学会不仅支持对"智力缺陷者"实施非自愿安乐死，还主张为富裕阶层提供资金以鼓励其多生育。虽然英国政府拒绝了优生教育学会关于强制绝育智力缺陷者的提议，但确实在 1913 年通过了《智力缺陷法案》，开始基于接近认知正常程度的标准实施大规模隔离。温斯顿·丘吉尔本人曾为该法案辩护称："智力缺陷阶层的反常且快速增长，加上节俭、进取的优良血统持续受限，构成了种族危机"。 2



In the United States, the Americanism ‘normalcy’ had been introduced to the broader public following the First World War, when ‘return to normalcy’ was used as Warren Harding’s 1920 presidential election campaign slogan (despite ‘normalcy’ not yet appearing in dictionaries). This period was accompanied – building on the cultural foundations laid by phrenology – by the further rise of Galtonian aspirations among members of the public. This can be seen in the ‘better baby’ or ‘fitter family’ contests that spread across the United States between the 1910s and 1930s. As Stern explains

在美国，"常态"这一美国主义词汇在第一次世界大战后被引入公众视野，当时"回归常态"被用作沃伦·哈定 1920 年总统竞选的口号（尽管"常态"一词尚未被收录进词典）。这一时期，在颅相学奠定的文化基础上，公众中高尔顿式理想进一步兴起。这体现在 1910 年代至 1930 年代间席卷美国的"更优婴儿"或"更健康家庭"竞赛中。正如斯特恩所解释的





the contests began at the Iowa State Fair in 1911 when clubwoman Mary T. Watts asked, ‘You are raising better cattle, better horses, and better hogs, why don’t you raise better babies?’ To judge infants like livestock, Watts and another rural reformer, Margaret Clark, devised scorecards that tallied level of physical health, anthropometric traits, and mental development.3

这些竞赛始于 1911 年的爱荷华州博览会，当时妇女俱乐部成员玛丽·T·瓦茨提出："你们在培育更优的牛、更优的马和更优的猪，为何不培育更优的婴儿？"为了像评判牲畜一样评判婴儿，瓦茨与另一位乡村改革者玛格丽特·克拉克设计了计分卡，用于统计身体健康水平、人体测量特征和智力发展状况。 3





As such contests spread, eugenics classes were also increasingly taught in many US universities, and eugenic policies were adopted in a variety of states. Women with intellectual disabilities – especially Black women – were forcibly sterilised, and people with cognitive disabilities were prevented from emigrating. Black disabled women in particular were seen not just as economic burdens but also threats to the purity of the white race.4

随着此类竞赛的蔓延，优生学课程也在美国许多大学中日益普及，各州纷纷采纳优生政策。智力障碍女性——尤其是黑人女性——被迫接受绝育手术，认知障碍者则被禁止移民。黑人残疾女性尤其被视为不仅是经济负担，更是对白人种族纯洁性的威胁。 4



It is important to note here that the ideology of normality was not only embraced on the right. Indeed, even Karl Marx’s concept of the ‘average worker’ was directly influenced by Quetelet.5 While Marx died in 1883 and would have never heard of eugenics, many on the left came to embrace Galton’s ideals. For instance, Sidney Webb, the co-founder of the London School of Economics, early member of the Fabian Society, and an influential socialist, lamented in 1896 about the ‘wrong production, both of commodities and of human beings; the preparation of senseless luxuries whilst there is need for more bread, and the breeding of degenerate hordes of a demoralized “residuum” unfit for social life’.6 The socialist and philosopher Bertrand Russell made similarly eugenicist proposals, writing in 1927 that by ‘sterilizing the feeble-minded of two generations, feeble-mindedness and idiocy could be almost stamped out’.7 Similarly, women’s rights campaigners such as Marie Stopes advocated compulsory sterilisation and suggested that birth control could improve British stock.8 In turn – as I shall return to later – eugenic ideas were also adopted in the Soviet Union, with the Russian Eugenics Society being founded in 1920 and Marxists such as Alexander Serebrovsky arguing for mass eugenics programmes.9

需要指出的是，对常态的意识形态的接纳并不仅限于右翼。事实上，就连卡尔·马克思的“普通工人”概念也直接受到了凯特莱的影响。 5 尽管马克思于 1883 年去世，从未听说过优生学，但左翼阵营中也有许多人开始接受高尔顿的理念。例如，伦敦政治经济学院的联合创始人、费边社早期成员、有影响力的社会主义者西德尼·韦伯在 1896 年曾哀叹“商品和人类的生产都出现了问题；在需要更多面包的时候却生产无意义的奢侈品，同时繁衍出道德败坏的‘残渣’群体，这些退化的群体不适合社会生活”。 6 社会主义者和哲学家伯特兰·罗素也提出了类似的优生学建议，他在 1927 年写道：“通过对两代智力低下者进行绝育，几乎可以消除智力低下和白痴现象。” 7 同样，玛丽·斯托普斯等女权运动倡导者也主张强制绝育，并认为节育可以改善英国的人口素质。 8 相应地——正如我稍后将再次提及的——优生学思想在苏联也得到了采纳，俄罗斯优生学会于 1920 年成立，像亚历山大·谢列布罗夫斯基这样的马克思主义者主张推行大规模优生计划。 9



Eugenicists drawing on the Galtonian research paradigm also had considerable influence over policy. For instance, following educational segregation in Britain, the post-war separation of children into three types of school – technical (for those good at practical trades), grammar (for those considered academic) and secondary modern (for everyone else) – was in significant part based on reasoning from Cyril Burt. Burt, who was a psychology professor and at one point a president of the British Psychological Society, was also a eugenicist who suggested that intelligence was innate and heritable. He claimed that children could be divided into three key kinds of intelligence, based on which British children of ‘normal’ ability were split into different kinds of schools in a system that still persists today – despite it later being found that Burt had fabricated the data from his twin studies.

遵循高尔顿研究范式的优生学家对政策也产生了相当大的影响。例如，在英国实行教育隔离之后，战后将儿童分为三类学校——技术学校（针对擅长实用技能者）、文法学校（针对被认为具有学术天赋者）和现代中学（针对其他所有人）——在很大程度上是基于西里尔·伯特的推理。伯特是一位心理学教授，曾担任英国心理学会主席，同时也是一位优生学家，他认为智力是天生的且可遗传。他声称儿童可分为三种主要智力类型，基于此，英国"正常"能力的儿童被分流到不同类型的学校，这一体系至今仍在延续——尽管后来发现伯特捏造了他的双胞胎研究数据。



Being endorsed across the political spectrum in the imperial core, eugenic ideology and policy were also exported to colonies. The historian Chloe Campbell has detailed how the British eugenics movement in particular became the ‘intellectual mother ship’10 for the spread of eugenic ideology and policy to colonies globally. This was often led by doctors and colonial officials who founded different eugenics organisations across the world. The specifics of their policies, however, depended on how local populations were racially positioned. For instance, the Kenyan Society for the Study of Race Improvement was founded in 1933. But in contrast to British eugenics – and despite the name of the society – the aim was to limit the population rather than to improve it. For since the Kenyan population was predominantly Black it was assumed by white officials that mental deficiency affected the entire population rather than only the working class and disabled.

在帝国核心地带获得跨政治光谱认可的同时，优生学意识形态与政策也被输出至殖民地。历史学家克洛伊·坎贝尔详细揭示了英国优生运动如何成为全球殖民地传播优生理念与政策的"思想母舰"。这股浪潮通常由医生和殖民官员引领，他们在世界各地建立了不同的优生组织。然而具体政策的制定，往往取决于当地族群在种族等级中的定位。例如 1933 年成立的肯尼亚种族改良研究会，尽管名称如此，其目标却与英国优生学背道而驰——并非改良人口而是限制增长。由于肯尼亚人口以黑人为主体，白人官员认定智力缺陷将遍及全体民众，而非仅局限于工人阶级与残障群体。



NAZI EUGENICS

纳粹优生学



Galton, after dedicating the last few decades of his life to eugenics, died in 1911. By this time, he had published over 340 books or articles and was a world-famous polymath. His writings on eugenics had inspired a global movement made up of the leading politicians, scientists, and philosophers of the generation. Still, he was worried that his ideas hadn’t yet reached a wide enough audience. In his final years he had thus been working on a novel titled Kantsaywhere, which was about a utopian society of the same name. This society was ruled through eugenic religion that focused on manipulating the sexual behaviours of its inhabitants. The whole society was dedicated to breeding fitter and smarter humans for the betterment of the race, thus improving human life in ways barely dreamed of prior to that time. It was Galton’s hope that his novel would spread these ideas even further among members of the wider population.

高尔顿在将生命的最后几十年奉献给优生学后，于 1911 年去世。此时，他已出版了超过 340 本书籍或文章，是一位世界闻名的博学家。他关于优生学的著作激发了一场由当时顶尖政治家、科学家和哲学家组成的全球性运动。尽管如此，他仍担心自己的思想尚未触及足够广泛的受众。因此，在晚年，他致力于创作一部名为《康塞维尔》的小说，描绘了一个同名的乌托邦社会。这个社会由一个专注于操控居民性行为的优生宗教所统治。整个社会致力于培育更健康、更聪明的人类，以促进种族的进步，从而以当时几乎无法想象的方式改善人类生活。高尔顿希望他的小说能在更广泛的人群中进一步传播这些理念。



Despite his great hopes, Galton did not live to see the fruition of authoritarian eugenic policy. And publishers showed little interest in his novel. Indeed, it was not published in his lifetime, and most of it was destroyed after his death by his daughter, perhaps due to its odd passages about sexual reproduction. But authoritarian eugenics did reach its logical endpoint just a mere few decades after Galton’s death. How it turned out, though, would be quite different to Galton’s utopian vision. For even though eugenic ideology had been devised in England and expanded in America, it was in Germany, following the rise of Hitler and national socialism, that it was finally implemented on an industrial scale.

尽管满怀厚望，高尔顿生前未能目睹威权优生政策的实现。出版商对他的小说也兴趣寥寥。事实上，这部作品在他有生之年未能付梓，其中大部分内容在他去世后被女儿销毁——或许是因为书中涉及生殖话题的怪异段落。然而，就在高尔顿离世后短短数十年间，威权优生学终究抵达了其逻辑终点。只是其发展轨迹，与高尔顿的乌托邦构想已相去甚远。尽管优生意识形态发轫于英国，兴盛于美国，但最终在希特勒与民族社会主义崛起的德国，才得以实现工业化规模的实践。



Born in 1889 in Austria-Hungary, Hitler was a strange child, full of resentment at others and seemingly unable to acknowledge his own inadequacies. He started out as a rather mediocre artist, studying in Vienna. Driven by his anti-Semitism and authoritarian nature, he was also increasingly drawn towards the new fascist politics that were emerging in Italy. At base, this was a petty-bourgeois movement that arose as a response to social crises of capitalism, and which then swung Italy and Germany towards imperialist reaction rather than towards revolution. This included further developing and implementing eugenic policy, this time on an industrial scale.

希特勒于 1889 年出生于奥匈帝国，是个古怪的孩子，满心怨恨他人，似乎无法承认自己的不足。他最初在维也纳学习艺术，成绩平平。受其反犹太主义和专制本性的驱使，他越来越被意大利新兴的法西斯政治所吸引。从根本上说，这是一场小资产阶级运动，是对资本主义社会危机的回应，随后将意大利和德国推向帝国主义反动而非革命。这包括进一步发展和实施优生政策，这次是在工业规模上。



Hitler himself wrote on a range of eugenic and racist ideas before becoming leader of the National Socialist German Workers’ Party in 1921. Driven by the ideologies of nationalism, racism, and eugenics, he eventually came to see society itself as an organism. In this view, a society’s individual members were understood as either stronger or weaker, compared to each other on a more or less Galtonian model. And because society itself was an organism, the weaker individuals were seen as weakening the whole organism, while the stronger members were seen as strengthening it. Those who were seen as unable to conform to Nazi racial and economic requirements – those whose minds and bodies fell outside the norm – were thus essentially seen as parasitic problems to be eliminated.

希特勒本人在 1921 年成为国家社会主义德国工人党领袖之前，就曾撰写过一系列优生学和种族主义思想。在民族主义、种族主义和优生学意识形态的驱动下，他最终将社会本身视为一个有机体。在这种观点中，社会个体成员被理解为或强或弱，彼此之间大致按照高尔顿模型进行比较。由于社会本身是一个有机体，较弱的个体被视为削弱整个有机体，而较强的成员则被视为增强它。因此，那些被认为无法符合纳粹种族和经济要求的人——那些思想和身体超出常规的人——基本上被视为需要消除的寄生问题。



Given these views, following Hitler’s election as Chancellor in 1933 and the establishment of his dictatorship shortly after, the Nazi Party began implementing authoritarian eugenic laws and policies. This included the ‘Law for the Prevention of Hereditarily Diseased Offspring’ of 1935, which prescribed compulsory sterilisation for thousands of neurodivergent people including those diagnosed with schizophrenia and cognitive disabilities. In turn, the Aktion T4 campaign between 1939 and 1945 went further, focusing on the mass murder of people deemed to impede the overall organismic functioning of the race.

基于这些观点，在希特勒于 1933 年当选总理并迅速建立独裁统治后，纳粹党开始推行威权优生法律与政策。这包括 1935 年颁布的《防止遗传病后代法》，该法规定对数千名神经殊异人士实施强制绝育，其中包括被诊断为精神分裂症和认知障碍者。随后，1939 年至 1945 年间实施的"T4 行动"更进一步，集中对被视为阻碍种族整体有机功能的人群进行大规模屠杀。



In retrospect this was all, quite clearly, based on racist and eugenicist ideology. Yet in many cases at the time the elimination was taken to be scientifically legitimised through Galtonian research methods and frameworks. For instance, as the historian Robert Proctor has detailed, research drawing on Galton’s twin studies technique was ‘lavishly funded’ and ‘purportedly demonstrated the heritability of everything from epilepsy, criminality, memory, and hernias to tuberculosis, cancer, schizophrenia, and divorce’.11 New Galtonian psychometric and psychological methods were also used to determine who was weaker or stronger and thus who should be able to live and reproduce.

回顾这一切，显然都是基于种族主义和优生学的意识形态。然而在当时，许多情况下，这种淘汰被认为是通过高尔顿的研究方法和框架得到了科学上的合法化。例如，正如历史学家罗伯特·普罗克特所详述的那样，借鉴高尔顿双胞胎研究技术的研究“获得了大量资助”，并“据称证明了从癫痫、犯罪倾向、记忆力、疝气到肺结核、癌症、精神分裂症乃至离婚等一切特征的遗传性”。 11 新的高尔顿式心理测量学和心理学方法也被用来判断谁更弱或更强，从而决定谁应该能够生存和繁衍。



In practice this helped justify how mentally ill and intellectually disabled children and adults were classified, assessed, sterilised, and, in many cases, murdered in huge numbers alongside Jews and other targets of Nazi eugenic policy. For instance, up to 269,500 people with schizophrenia alone are thought to have been sterilised or murdered in Germany between 1939 and 1945.12 Mothers of cognitively disabled children were told they were ‘useless eaters’, while doctors were required to report congenital impairments ranging from deafness to Down’s syndrome. As Robison13 notes, parents ‘were encouraged to place those children in residential clinics, for the good of the family and the state. Once institutionalized, the children were systematically killed by poison, starvation, or exposure’. This was framed by Nazi doctors and politicians as a matter of ‘racial hygiene’ and as necessary for lifting the ‘national burden’ that the Nazi Party associated with disability.

在实践中，这为将精神疾病和智力残障的儿童与成人进行分类、评估、绝育，并在许多情况下与犹太人及其他纳粹优生政策目标群体一同大规模屠杀提供了正当性依据。例如，据估计在 1939 年至 1945 年间，仅精神分裂症患者就有多达 269,500 人在德国被绝育或杀害。 12 认知残障儿童的母亲被告知她们的孩子是"无用的食客"，而医生则被要求上报从耳聋到唐氏综合征等各种先天性损伤。正如罗宾逊 13 所指出的，父母"被鼓励将这些孩子送入寄宿诊所，为了家庭和国家的利益。一旦被收容，这些孩子就会通过投毒、饥饿或暴露在恶劣环境中被系统性地杀害"。纳粹医生和政治家将这种行为包装为"种族卫生"问题，并声称这对于减轻纳粹党与残障相关联的"国家负担"是必要的。



Indeed, it was in Nazi-occupied Austria that autism was coined as a diagnosis. While the term had been coined by the eugenicist and psychiatrist Eugene Bleuler in 1911, Bleuler only meant it to refer to a temporary symptom of schizophrenia. It was only under Nazi rule, in the work of Hans Asperger in the 1930s and 1940s, that those who came to be called autistic were singled out as having a unique way of being. During a war period where men were expected to express a ‘soldier mentality’ and to be part of the group, boys who failed to fit this economic requirement were singled out as pathological (it was mostly boys who got the diagnosis) and were baptised with a new name: autism. Those women who were diagnosed were also singled out if they had intellectual disabilities, since they were not seen as fit to reproduce. Hence it was in significant part Nazi gender norms, determined by ideological and economic factors, that first allowed the autism spectrum to manifest as a distinct way of being.14 In this context Hans Asperger and other medics began dividing autistics up into those deemed to have potential worth to the Third Reich given their purportedly strong logical capacities, and those who were to be sterilised or killed along with countless other mad and disabled targets.

确实，正是在纳粹占领下的奥地利，"孤独谱系"这一诊断术语被创造出来。虽然这个词由优生学家兼精神病学家尤金·布洛伊勒于 1911 年首创，但布洛伊勒仅用它来指代精神分裂症的一种暂时性症状。直到纳粹统治时期，在汉斯·阿斯伯格于 20 世纪 30 至 40 年代的工作中，那些后来被称为"孤独谱系"的人才被单独区分出来，被视为拥有一种独特的存在方式。在战争时期，男性被期望表现出"士兵心态"并融入集体，而那些未能符合这一经济要求的男孩（当时被诊断的主要是男孩）被单独列为病态，并被赋予了一个新名称：孤独谱系。那些被诊断的女性，如果同时存在智力障碍，也会被单独区分，因为她们被认为不适合生育。因此，在很大程度上，正是由意识形态和经济因素决定的纳粹性别规范，首次使得孤独谱系作为一种独特的存在方式得以显现。 在此背景下，汉斯·阿斯伯格及其他医疗人员开始将孤独谱系人士划分为两类：一类因其据称强大的逻辑能力而被认为对第三帝国具有潜在价值；另一类则与无数其他被视为疯狂或残疾的目标一样，将被绝育或杀害。



These earlier eugenics policies have been described as ‘the first chapter’ of the Holocaust, where around 6 million Jews were murdered in line with Nazi racial ideology.15 This was only halted by the allied victory in 1945. Prior to this, many British and American eugenicists had watched the eugenic experiment of Nazi Germany with great interest. But as the full extent of the horrors of the Holocaust increasingly came to light, support for authoritarian eugenic policies sharply declined in liberal societies. At the same time, Kraepelinian biological psychiatry also came to be seen as tainted through its association with Nazi eugenics. Because of this, Freudian psychoanalysis and behaviourism – the main alternatives to biological psychiatry available at the time – became dominant in US and European psychiatry in the 1950s. It is to these, and in turn the critique from anti-psychiatry critics, that we shall turn in the following chapters.

这些早期的优生学政策被描述为大屠杀的"第一章"，在此期间约有 600 万犹太人根据纳粹种族意识形态被杀害。 15 直到 1945 年盟军胜利，这一暴行才被制止。在此之前，许多英美优生学家曾对纳粹德国的优生实验抱有浓厚兴趣。但随着大屠杀恐怖真相的逐渐揭露，自由主义社会对威权优生政策的支持急剧下降。与此同时，克雷佩林生物精神病学也因其与纳粹优生学的关联而蒙上污名。正因如此，当时生物精神病学的主要替代方案——弗洛伊德精神分析学派和行为主义学派——在 1950 年代成为欧美精神病学的主流。我们将在后续章节中探讨这些理论，以及反精神病学批评家对其的批判。



THE PATHOLOGY PARADIGM

病理学范式



I have outlined the intellectual and social history surrounding the mental health and normality concepts up until the mid-twentieth century. In theories of health, the core shifts I have detailed are the move from equilibrium to normal state conceptions of health and the Galtonian fusing of Darwin and normality to begin ranking populations. This happened within the rise of capitalism, which brought new cognitive hierarchies and accumulation of wealth by those whose cognitive dispositions fit this new mode of economic organisation. At the same time, new statistical methods and the mechanistic understanding of the body and mind allowed this to be scientifically legitimised.

我已概述了直至二十世纪中叶围绕心理健康与常态概念的思想史和社会史。在健康理论中，我所详述的核心转变是从平衡观转向健康常态观，以及高尔顿将达尔文思想与常态概念融合，开始对人群进行等级划分。这一切发生在资本主义兴起的背景下，资本主义带来了新的认知等级制度，并使那些认知倾向适应这种新经济组织模式的人积累了财富。与此同时，新的统计方法以及对身心的机械论理解，使这一切获得了科学上的合法性。



The core assumptions of the pathology paradigm are that mental and cognitive functioning are individual and based on natural abilities, and can be ranked in relation to a statistical norm across the species. And while there were earlier notions of the mean understanding and normal body, I locate Galton as the founder of the pathology paradigm proper. Walker describes the pathology paradigm as being the place where the neurotypical mind became ‘enthroned as the “normal” ideal against which all other types of minds are measured’.16 And it was also with Galton that this, and mass normalisation, was formalised.

病理学范式的核心假设是，心理和认知功能是个体性的，基于自然能力，并且可以相对于物种的统计规范进行排序。尽管早先已有关于平均理解和正常身体的概念，但我将高尔顿视为病理学范式本身的创始人。沃克将病理学范式描述为神经典型心智被“奉为‘正常’理想，所有其他类型的心智都以此为标准来衡量”的地方。 16 也正是通过高尔顿，这一点以及大规模正常化被正式确立。



I also want to be clear here that, although I have focused on authoritarian eugenics, I do not mean to claim that eugenic theory is synonymous with pathology paradigm theory. As we have seen, Galton developed the basis of the paradigm several decades before he came up with the further notion of eugenics. Thus, while they are closely intertwined and grew together, they are not identical. The difference is that the pathology paradigm does not necessarily commit to the idea that the race or species can be improved at the group level. It only shares the underlying idea that we can rank populations in terms of mental abilities, and that higher in the ranking is more desirable. They are, then, closely interrelated but also distinct. This is important to recognise because there are countless, more or less subtle, ways this theory and ideology manifests in the Empire of Normality, and yet which are not based on an explicit attempt to improve the race or species. In fact, following the allied victory, many eugenics professors and researchers simply switched departments or roles, but carried on much as before. ‘Eugenics’ became ‘genetics’, for instance, and still focused on eliminating abnormalities even if this was framed as an individual medical problem more than an issue of race.

在此我也要明确指出，尽管我重点讨论了威权优生学，但这并不意味着优生学理论与病理学范式理论是同义词。正如我们所看到的，高尔顿在提出优生学这一进一步概念之前的几十年里，就已经奠定了该范式的基础。因此，尽管它们紧密交织、共同发展，但并非完全相同。区别在于，病理学范式并不一定承诺种族或物种可以在群体层面得到改善。它只共享一个基本理念：我们可以根据心智能力对人群进行排序，并且排名越高越理想。因此，它们密切相关但又有所区别。认识到这一点很重要，因为这种理论和意识形态在《正常帝国》中以无数或微妙或明显的方式表现出来，而这些方式并非基于明确改善种族或物种的企图。事实上，在盟军胜利后，许多优生学教授和研究人员只是更换了部门或角色，但工作内容基本照旧。 例如，“优生学”演变为“遗传学”，其核心仍在于消除异常，尽管这更多地被包装为个体医学问题，而非种族议题。



Indeed, as we shall see in the following chapters, a new Fordist, and then neoliberal, ideology of normality that became dominant in the twentieth century fused with later iterations of the pathology paradigm across a variety of sciences. While these would not, in most cases, be based on any conscious quest to improve the race, they would still be grounded in the same metaphysical assumptions as the earlier pathology paradigm. As such they would continue to reify even more restricted cognitive hierarchies that would manifest as capitalism continued to intensify and develop.

事实上，正如我们将在后续章节中看到的，一种新的福特主义，以及后来的新自由主义正常性意识形态，在二十世纪占据主导地位，并与病理学范式在多种科学领域的后续迭代相融合。尽管在大多数情况下，这些理论并非基于任何有意识地改善种族的追求，但它们仍然建立在与早期病理学范式相同的形而上学假设之上。因此，它们将继续物化更为狭隘的认知等级体系，这种等级体系将随着资本主义的持续强化和发展而显现。



---

Empire of Normality



5



The myths of anti-psychiatry

反精神病学的迷思



One impact of Nazism was that a great many Jews and other targets of Nazi ideology fled the European continent in the 1930s. This mass exodus included some who were or would go on to become leading artists, philosophers, or scientists, who went to Britain, the United States, and elsewhere. Our own story now turns to two such men who, separately, fled Europe due to the Nazi threat. When each emigrated in the late 1930s, one was then an already famous neurologist and therapist whose ideas would shortly come to dominate American psychiatry. The other was a then-unknown teenage student. Yet, in time, he would go on to be among the most influential critics of the former’s approach. And in pursuing this he would help found the philosophy of a movement that would bring psychiatry itself to its knees in the 1970s.

纳粹主义的一个影响是，在 20 世纪 30 年代，大量犹太人及其他纳粹意识形态的迫害对象逃离了欧洲大陆。这场大规模流亡中包括一些当时或后来成为杰出艺术家、哲学家或科学家的人，他们前往英国、美国及其他地区。我们的故事现在转向两位因纳粹威胁而各自逃离欧洲的人物。当他们在 20 世纪 30 年代末移民时，一位已是著名的神经学家和治疗师，其思想很快将主导美国精神病学；另一位则是当时默默无闻的青少年学生。然而，随着时间的推移，他将成为对前者方法最具影响力的批评者之一。在这一过程中，他协助奠定了一场哲学运动的基础，而这股力量将在 20 世纪 70 年代使精神病学本身遭受重创。



The elder of the two was Sigmund Freud. Born in 1856 in the town of Freiburg, then part of the Austrian empire, Freud was brought up by his father, a modest wool merchant, and his mother, an intelligent and quick-witted housewife. Freud himself was a diligent student and thus able to train as a physician and neurologist at the University of Vienna. He then worked on a range of research projects after graduating. This included early experiments on the therapeutic effects of cocaine and hypnosis. But it was his development of ‘psychoanalysis’ that brought his lasting fame. This was a theory and method for analysing what Freud called the ‘unconscious’ mind, which Freud used to develop a ‘talking cure’ for neuroses of the psyche. It was this that would later become a dominant school in psychiatry and psychology across much of the world.

两人中较年长的是西格蒙德·弗洛伊德。他于 1856 年出生在弗赖堡镇，当时属于奥地利帝国。弗洛伊德由父亲——一位朴素的羊毛商人——和母亲——一位聪慧机敏的家庭主妇——抚养长大。弗洛伊德本人勤奋好学，得以在维也纳大学接受医师和神经学家的训练。毕业后，他从事了一系列研究工作，包括早期关于可卡因和催眠治疗效果的实验。但真正让他声名远扬的是他创立的“精神分析学”。这是一套分析弗洛伊德所称“潜意识”的理论与方法，弗洛伊德借此发展出针对心理神经症的“谈话疗法”。正是这一理论后来成为全球大部分地区精神病学和心理学领域的主导学派。



The younger of the two, Thomas Szasz, never met Freud, but spent much of his life grappling with the former’s thought and work. Born in 1920 in Budapest in what had then just become the Kingdom of Hungary to an upper-middle-class family, Szasz was brought up by his father, who ran a thriving agricultural business, his mother, and his governess. This was, at least, until the family had to flee the rise of Nazism to the US in 1938. Szasz was thus 18 when he moved across the Atlantic, just as Freud was living out his final months in London. And so it was in America that Szasz would study medicine, build a life, and, in time, become among psychiatry’s most influential critics.

两人中较年轻的那位，托马斯·萨兹，从未见过弗洛伊德，却耗费大半生钻研这位前辈的思想与著作。萨兹于 1920 年出生在布达佩斯——当时刚成为匈牙利王国的城市——一个中上阶层家庭，由经营着兴旺农业生意的父亲、母亲及家庭女教师共同抚养长大。这样的生活至少持续到 1938 年，因纳粹主义抬头，全家被迫逃往美国。横渡大西洋时萨兹刚满 18 岁，而彼时弗洛伊德正在伦敦度过人生最后数月。正是在美国，萨兹攻读医学、安身立命，并最终成为精神病学领域最具影响力的批评者之一。



Today, although much of his work is now rejected, Freud is known as the father of psychoanalysis and psychotherapy. He is also a major figure in the history of psychiatry and psychology. By contrast, Szasz is known as the most influential of all ‘anti-psychiatrists’. While he rejected the term himself, ‘anti-psychiatry’ is usually used to refer to a group of rogue psychiatrists and social theorists who challenged psychiatric pathologisation in the 1960s and 1970s. These included Ronald Laing, the Scottish psychiatrist who argued that schizophrenia is a reasonable reaction to distressing family dynamics, the Canadian sociologist Erving Goffman, who described asylums as ‘total institutions’ and diagnoses as ‘labels’, and the French philosopher Michel Foucault, whose work we have already mentioned.

如今，尽管弗洛伊德的许多理论已被摒弃，他仍被尊为精神分析与心理治疗之父，同时也是精神病学与心理学史上的重要人物。相比之下，萨兹则以最具影响力的"反精神病学"代表人物而闻名。虽然他本人拒绝这一标签，但"反精神病学"通常指代二十世纪六七十年代挑战精神病学病理化的一批叛逆精神病学家与社会理论家。其中包括苏格兰精神病学家罗纳德·莱恩——他认为精神分裂症是对痛苦家庭动态的合理反应；加拿大社会学家欧文·戈夫曼——他将精神病院描述为"全控机构"，将诊断称为"标签"；以及我们已提及的法国哲学家米歇尔·福柯。



While Szasz and Freud differed fundamentally in many commitments, they nonetheless shared a great deal beyond their religious background and profession. Both became influential for the counter-cultural movements in the late 1960s. They each also developed important theories relating to the mind, mental health, and society at large. Indeed, the ideas or arguments of each have also become so influential they are echoed daily today, often by people who are barely aware of their origins. And they have also each been part of an ongoing mass conflict between the state and those deemed mentally ill or disabled. To understand this, it is thus to Freud, Szasz, and the broader movements they are symbolic of, that our story now turns.

尽管萨兹和弗洛伊德在许多信念上存在根本分歧，但除了宗教背景和职业之外，他们仍有许多共同之处。两人都对 20 世纪 60 年代末的反文化运动产生了重要影响。他们各自还发展了关于心灵、心理健康和整个社会的重要理论。事实上，他们各自的思想或论点至今仍具有深远影响，每天都能听到回响，而许多人甚至不清楚这些思想的来源。此外，他们都曾卷入国家与被认定为精神疾病或残疾者之间持续的大规模冲突之中。为了理解这一点，我们的故事现在转向弗洛伊德、萨兹以及他们所象征的更广泛运动。



THE FREUDIAN TRIUMPH

弗洛伊德主义的胜利



As discussed in the previous chapter, Kraepelinian biological psychiatry was widely seen as tainted in liberal circles following increased awareness of the Holocaust. Eugenicists slunk away to genetics and psychology departments and rebranded their work without reference to the improvement of races. By contrast, Freud was Jewish and had thus fled from Vienna to England to escape persecution from the Nazis, who had detested his work given their anti-Semitism. As such his work was not tainted by an association with Nazism. Moreover, during a period of mass collective trauma, Freud’s work was also useful for understanding the kind of psychological damage that followed the horrors of the Second World War. For instead of examining brains and using statistical analyses, Freud was interested in human suffering and how it might be explained in relation to unconscious drives, trauma, or early childhood experiences.

正如前一章所讨论的，随着对纳粹大屠杀认识的加深，克雷佩林式的生物精神病学在自由主义圈子里被广泛视为受到玷污。优生学家们悄然转向遗传学和心理学系，并重新包装他们的工作，不再提及种族改良。相比之下，弗洛伊德是犹太人，因此从维也纳逃到英国以躲避纳粹的迫害，而纳粹因其反犹太主义而憎恶他的工作。因此，他的工作并未因与纳粹主义的关联而受到玷污。此外，在大规模集体创伤时期，弗洛伊德的理论也有助于理解第二次世界大战恐怖之后出现的心理创伤。因为弗洛伊德关注的不是检查大脑或使用统计分析，而是人类的痛苦，以及如何通过无意识驱力、创伤或早期童年经历来解释这种痛苦。



Indeed, not only was the Freudian approach seemingly useful for healing psychological problems. It was also useful for understanding society more broadly, as Freud himself first demonstrated in his 1929 book Civilization and its Discontents, where he examined the tension between the societal need for conformity and the individual sexual and aggressive instincts. Building on this, in a seminal 1933 book titled The Mass Psychology of Fascism,1 Freud’s follower Wilhelm Reich argued that Freudian theory might also be able to explain the rise of totalitarianism. Some thus came to believe that psychoanalysis might even help the rest of the world avoid repeating the horrors of the Holocaust. Others still, such as Freud’s nephew and the father of public relations, Edward Bernays, drew on Freud’s theories to help sell products and influence public perception. Bernays unashamedly defended what he described as the scientific development of ‘propaganda’ methods, which was helpful for capitalists and governments alike. Given such developments – alongside behaviourism, as we will see – the Freudian approach was able to quickly become a leading model in psychology and psychiatry. This was for understanding not just mental illness, but also child development and the human psyche much more broadly.

确实，弗洛伊德的方法不仅看似有助于解决心理问题，更在更广泛的社会理解层面展现出价值。弗洛伊德本人在 1929 年的著作《文明及其不满》中首次论证了这一点，探讨了社会对一致性的需求与个体性及攻击本能之间的张力。在此基础上，弗洛伊德的追随者威廉·赖希在 1933 年的开创性著作《法西斯主义的大众心理学》中提出，弗洛伊德理论或许也能解释极权主义的兴起。因此，一些人开始相信精神分析甚至可能帮助世界避免重蹈大屠杀的覆辙。另一些人，如弗洛伊德的侄子、公共关系之父爱德华·伯奈斯，则借鉴弗洛伊德的理论来推销产品和影响公众认知。伯奈斯毫不掩饰地为他所谓的“宣传”方法的科学发展辩护，认为这对资本家和政府都有益处。鉴于这些发展——以及我们将看到的行为主义——弗洛伊德的方法得以迅速成为心理学和精神病学的主导模式。 这不仅是为了理解精神疾病，也是为了更广泛地理解儿童发展和人类心理。



When it came to psychiatry, while there were only a small number of immigrant psychoanalysts in the United States in 1940, the Freudian approach would become the dominant school by 1950. Psychoanalysts came to run most university psychiatry departments, and psychoanalytic theory quickly came to influence other fields as well as art and culture. At the same time, partly after having dropped a nuclear bomb on Hiroshima, the United States was also undeniably the new world superpower. This power was in turn greatly increased in 1948, when the US donated over 13 billion dollars to help rebuild much of Europe and Turkey in exchange for increased influence and economic dominance. As such the scientific and cultural influence of US psychiatry was increasingly significant as the old European empires crumbled. Given the heightened influence of American imperialism, psychoanalysis established an at least temporary hegemony not just in the US but also far beyond.

在精神病学领域，尽管 1940 年美国只有少数移民精神分析师，但到 1950 年，弗洛伊德学派已成为主导流派。精神分析师开始掌管大多数大学的精神病学系，精神分析理论也迅速影响了其他领域以及艺术文化。与此同时，美国在向广岛投下原子弹后，无可否认地成为了新的世界超级大国。这一实力在 1948 年得到极大增强，当时美国捐赠超过 130 亿美元帮助重建欧洲大部分地区和土耳其，以换取更大的影响力和经济主导地位。随着旧欧洲帝国的衰落，美国精神病学的科学和文化影响力日益显著。鉴于美帝国主义影响力的提升，精神分析不仅在美国，而且在更广泛的地区建立了至少是暂时的霸权。



Interestingly, while he did rely on Darwin for his understanding of instincts and drives, to some extent Freud briefly brought back aspects of an equilibrium conception of mental health. This is because – likely inspired by similar ideas from Ancient Egypt – Freud saw mental illness as stemming from the upset equilibrium between conscious and unconscious drives. For instance, certain drives might be repressed due to societal pressures or as a result of traumatic experiences, in ways that led to internal disharmony and thus psychic suffering. In making this move Freudian psychoanalysis and its offshoots brought great insights that had been missed in biocentric approaches. These were mainly regarding the workings of the psyche, the role of unconscious drives and instincts, and on the matter of childhood development and interpersonal dynamics.

有趣的是，尽管弗洛伊德确实借鉴了达尔文对本能和驱力的理解，但在某种程度上，他短暂地恢复了心理健康平衡观的某些方面。这很可能是因为——或许受到古埃及类似观念的启发——弗洛伊德将精神疾病视为意识与无意识驱力之间平衡被打破的结果。例如，某些驱力可能因社会压力或创伤经历而受到压抑，从而导致内在的不和谐，进而引发心理痛苦。通过这一转向，弗洛伊德精神分析及其分支带来了生物中心主义方法所忽视的重要洞见，主要涉及心理运作机制、无意识驱力和本能的作用，以及童年发展和人际动态等方面。



This also brought a new therapeutic approach. Freud himself spent much time with patients helping them talk through their problems, hoping to untangle their internal conflicts. He then reported on and analysed these cases in his writings, which were widely read among clinicians and members of the educated public alike. In time, the Freudian approach came to help many suffering people, by introducing new frameworks and vocabularies alongside talking therapies that allowed people to confront traumas, help make sense of early childhood problems, and work through strained family relationships.

这也催生了一种新的治疗方法。弗洛伊德本人花费大量时间与患者交谈，帮助他们梳理问题，试图解开他们内心的冲突。随后，他在著作中记录并分析了这些案例，这些作品在临床医生和受过教育的公众中广为流传。随着时间的推移，弗洛伊德的方法通过引入新的框架和词汇，结合谈话疗法，帮助了许多受苦的人们，使他们能够直面创伤、理解童年早期的问题，并处理紧张的家庭关系。



Despite Freud’s great insights, the dominance of his followers was not destined to last. It was not just that many of his followers became dogmatists in their teaching and practice, especially after Freud’s death in 1939. And neither was it just that the efficacy of psychoanalytic intervention had not been established through rigorous scientific testing. While these were genuine problems, it was also that Freud himself had broadened the boundaries of mental illness in such a way that ended up helping psychiatry expand its sphere of control. In his 1906 book The Psychopathology of Everyday Life, for instance, Freud suggested that pretty much everyone was somewhat neurotic, and that this could be detected in ordinary things such as forgetting words or unintended movements.2 This meant that the psychoanalyst was now placed to heal a great variety of problems previously considered part of the ordinary suffering of daily life, and more the domain of the priest than the medic.

尽管弗洛伊德有着深刻的洞见，但其追随者的主导地位并未注定长久。这不仅仅是因为许多追随者在教学和实践中变得教条主义，尤其是在 1939 年弗洛伊德去世之后；也不仅仅是因为精神分析干预的有效性尚未通过严格的科学测试得到证实。虽然这些都是真实存在的问题，但弗洛伊德本人也拓宽了精神疾病的边界，这种方式最终帮助精神病学扩大了其控制范围。例如，在他 1906 年的著作《日常生活的心理病理学》中，弗洛伊德提出，几乎每个人都有一定程度的神经症，这可以通过诸如忘记词语或无意识的动作等日常事物中察觉出来。这意味着精神分析师现在被置于治疗各种问题的位置，这些问题以前被认为是日常生活普通痛苦的一部分，更多属于牧师而非医生的领域。



Alongside this broadening and blurring of the boundaries between the worried well and the unwell, many American psychoanalytic psychiatrists later overtook the running of the asylums without reforming them. Many barbarous practices and abuses continued much as before. And so for critics of the asylums, psychoanalysts became complicit in an existing state carceral system. At the same time, it was becoming increasingly apparent that patriarchal, racialised, and heteronormative power relations manifested in who was deemed mentally ill as well as how their problems were interpreted. Women were pathologised as ‘hysterical’ for challenging patriarchy, while Black men and women were labelled as having a ‘protest psychosis’ for resisting racism. Critics of this system began to analyse the conceptual and scientific basis of psychoanalysis itself, and to argue that it lacked sound scientific grounding or evidence.

随着担忧健康者与不健康者之间界限的扩大和模糊，许多美国精神分析精神病学家后来接管了精神病院的运营，却未对其进行改革。许多野蛮的做法和虐待行为依然如故。因此，对于精神病院的批评者来说，精神分析学家成为了现有国家监禁体系的共谋。与此同时，父权制、种族化和异性恋规范权力关系在谁被视为精神疾病患者以及如何解释他们的问题上表现得越来越明显。女性因挑战父权制而被病理化为“歇斯底里”，而黑人男女则因反抗种族主义而被贴上“抗议性精神病”的标签。这一体系的批评者开始分析精神分析本身的概念和科学基础，并认为它缺乏坚实的科学依据或证据。



By the end of the 1960s psychiatric survivors, health professionals, researchers, patients, and members of the broader public would thus end up becoming increasingly sceptical of Freudian psychiatry. In time, all this disquiet came to be captured in the anti-psychiatry movement, which – especially through the work of Szasz – brought a fierce critique of not just psychoanalytic psychiatry, but also of the very concept of ‘mental illness’ upon which they took psychiatry’s power to be founded.

到 20 世纪 60 年代末，精神病幸存者、医疗专业人员、研究者、患者以及更广泛的公众因此对弗洛伊德式精神病学日益怀疑。最终，所有这些不安情绪汇聚成了反精神病学运动——尤其是通过萨斯的工作——该运动不仅对精神分析精神病学提出了猛烈批判，更对"精神疾病"这一概念本身发起了抨击，而精神病学的权力正是建立在这一概念之上。



SZASZ ON THE ‘MYTH’ OF MENTAL ILLNESS

萨斯论"精神疾病"的"迷思"



To understand this in more detail, let us return to 1938 – one year prior to Freud’s death – when Szasz arrived in the United States. Once settled, Szasz studied physics and then medicine at the University of Cincinnati, graduating at the top of his class. Even as a student, Szasz later reported, he was already sceptical that psychiatry was a genuine branch of medicine. As a committed libertarian he was also firmly against involuntary confinement and much of what went on in the asylums.

为了更详细地理解这一点，让我们回到 1938 年——弗洛伊德逝世的前一年——当时萨斯抵达美国。安顿下来后，萨斯在辛辛那提大学先后攻读物理学和医学，以班级第一名的成绩毕业。据萨斯后来回忆，早在学生时代，他就已怀疑精神病学是否真正属于医学的分支。作为一名坚定的自由意志主义者，他也坚决反对非自愿拘禁以及精神病院里发生的诸多行径。



Despite his reservations, Szasz initially wanted to be an independent psychoanalyst. While he did not see psychoanalysis as a branch of science or medicine, he made a sharp distinction between what he called ‘consensual psychoanalysis’ and ‘pseudo-medical psychoanalysis’. The former, in his own words, was a kind of ‘confidential dialogue that often helps people resolve their personal problems and may help them improve their ability to cope’.3 By contrast, ‘pseudo-medical psychoanalysis’ wrongly purported to be a scientific intervention and was used to justify locking patients up against their will.4 This latter approach, which positioned clients as patients in need of treatment, was seen by Szasz as a form of social control masquerading as science.

尽管有所保留，萨兹最初仍希望成为一名独立的精神分析师。他虽不将精神分析视为科学或医学的分支，却对所谓的"共识性精神分析"与"伪医学精神分析"作出了明确区分。用他自己的话说，前者是一种"私密对话，常能帮助人们解决个人问题，并可能提升其应对能力"。 3 相比之下，"伪医学精神分析"则错误地宣称自己是科学干预手段，并被用来为违背患者意愿的监禁行为辩护。 4 这种将来访者定位为需要治疗的患者的做法，被萨兹视为伪装成科学的社会控制形式。



Szasz may not have believed psychiatry was a medical science, but he nonetheless had to complete his medical training to qualify to practice private psychoanalysis. He thus took up a psychiatry residency at Cincinnati General Hospital and then worked for several further years at the Chicago Institute for Psychoanalysis. During this period, he kept his views about psychiatry quiet in the knowledge that speaking out could damage his career prospects. Following this he joined the State University of New York as a professor in 1956, where he would work for the rest of his career. This also gave him the stability needed to begin writing, and in time, start publishing his critique of psychiatry.

萨兹可能并不认为精神病学是一门医学科学，但他仍需完成医学培训才有资格从事私人精神分析工作。因此，他在辛辛那提总医院接受了精神病学住院医师培训，随后又在芝加哥精神分析研究所工作了数年。在此期间，他对自己关于精神病学的观点保持沉默，因为他深知公开表态可能会损害自己的职业前景。此后，他于 1956 年加入纽约州立大学担任教授，并在此度过了余下的职业生涯。这份工作也为他提供了开始写作并最终发表对精神病学批判所需的稳定环境。



To his students and colleagues, he quickly became known as a charismatic lecturer with a sharp wit. But he only achieved fame – or notoriety – with his 1960 article ‘The Myth of Mental Illness’, which he developed into a best-selling book of the same title the following year. While he had published a more minor critique several years earlier, it was here that his iconoclastic analysis of his own profession, and, implicitly, many of his former mentors and his current colleagues, was unleashed. These early works outlined the core arguments that he continued to develop for the rest of his life, and which have underpinned much critique of psychiatry since this time.

在学生和同事眼中，他很快以机智敏锐、富有魅力的讲师形象闻名。但直到 1960 年发表《精神疾病的神话》一文后，他才真正声名鹊起——或者说恶名远扬。次年他将此文扩展成同名畅销书出版。虽然几年前他曾发表过一篇影响力较小的批评文章，但正是在这部作品中，他对自身职业——以及隐含地对许多昔日导师与现任同僚——展开了颠覆性的剖析。这些早期著作勾勒出他毕生不断完善的核心论点，也为此后对精神病学的诸多批判奠定了基石。



Szasz’s argument5 had a historical aspect and a philosophical aspect, and it will be useful to consider both. His historical claim was that ‘mental illness’ was a metaphor, proposed in the 1800s, that, over time, psychiatry had come to forget was a metaphor. Given this error, psychiatry had come to respond to mental illness as if it was a genuine medical issue. First, they thus tried to locate and treat it in the brain, even though there was no evidence that most mental illnesses were biologically grounded. In turn, they had conceptualised talking therapies as if they were medical, when in fact they were nothing more than forms of social support. While this could sometimes be useful, Szasz argued, it had come to give psychiatrists an unjustified social positioning that allowed them to imprison people for crimes they had not even yet committed, and may not ever do so. As such, for Szasz, over time the idea of mental illness, and the various specific psychiatric diagnoses such as hysteria or schizophrenia, had come to legitimise psychiatry as a form of state control by bestowing it with a medical respectability it did not deserve.

萨兹的论点包含历史层面和哲学层面，两者都值得探讨。他的历史主张是，“精神疾病”是一个在 19 世纪提出的隐喻，而随着时间的推移，精神病学逐渐忘记了这个隐喻。由于这一错误，精神病学开始将精神疾病当作真正的医学问题来应对。首先，他们试图在大脑中定位并治疗它，尽管没有证据表明大多数精神疾病具有生物学基础。相应地，他们将谈话疗法概念化为医学治疗，而实际上这些疗法不过是社会支持的形式。萨兹认为，虽然这有时可能有用，但它赋予了精神病学家一种不合理的社会地位，使他们能够以人们尚未犯下、甚至可能永远不会犯下的罪行来监禁他们。因此，在萨兹看来，随着时间的推移，精神疾病的概念以及诸如歇斯底里或精神分裂症等各种具体的精神病学诊断，通过赋予精神病学不应有的医学尊重，使其作为一种国家控制形式合法化。



In turn, Szasz’s philosophical critique aimed to render the very concept of ‘mental illness’ incoherent and invalid. Importantly – and in stark contrast to subsequent neurodiversity proponents – Szasz did not challenge the concept of biological or neurological normality in his critique of mental illness. In fact, the assumption that the concept of biological normality was wholly scientific and objective precisely underpinned his critique. His argument was only against the ‘mental’ part of mental illness or disorder. He held that if there was no known neurological or otherwise biological abnormality underpinning the ‘mental’ problem, then the problem is not a medical problem, and is only a ‘problem in living’.

反过来，萨斯（Szasz）的哲学批判旨在使“精神疾病”这一概念本身变得不连贯且无效。重要的是——与后来的神经多样性倡导者形成鲜明对比——萨斯在其对精神疾病的批判中并未挑战生物或神经学上的“正常”概念。事实上，正是基于生物正常性概念完全是科学且客观的这一假设，才支撑了他的批判。他的论点仅针对精神疾病或障碍中的“精神”部分。他认为，如果“精神”问题背后没有已知的神经学或其他生物学异常作为支撑，那么这个问题就不是医学问题，而仅仅是“生活中的问题”。



Szasz’s argument thus essentially rested on a comparison between what he took to be objective bodily medicine and value-laden psychiatry. In his own words, any legitimate ‘concept of illness’ standardly ‘implies deviation from a clearly defined norm. In the case of physical illness the norm is the structural and functional integrity of the human body’.6 In particular he took cellular pathology resulting from lesion as the archetypical form of medical abnormality. Because he saw the idea of the normal body to be timeless and objectively grounded, Szasz posited that somatic medicine and its conceptions of normality were ‘free from wide differences of ethical value’.7

因此，萨兹的论点本质上建立在他所认为的客观身体医学与充满价值判断的精神病学之间的比较之上。用他自己的话说，任何合法的“疾病概念”通常“都意味着偏离了明确定义的规范。在身体疾病的情况下，规范是人体的结构和功能完整性”。 6 特别是，他将由病变引起的细胞病理学视为医学异常的原型形式。由于他认为正常身体的概念是永恒且客观的，萨兹假设躯体医学及其正常性概念“不受广泛伦理价值差异的影响”。 7



By contrast, he argued, what we call ‘mental illness’ was importantly different to bodily illness. This was because, he wrote, the ‘norm from which deviation is measured whenever one speaks of a mental illness is a psychosocial and ethical one’.8 That is, whether a psychiatrist thought someone was mad or not would essentially come down to their subjective judgement, not an objective biological test. Hence in this argument, we can see that psychoanalytic psychiatry was based on a myth – the myth that mental illness is genuine illness – because psychoanalytic judgements about illness are relatively lacking in objectivity when compared to judgement about normality in bodily medicine.9

相比之下，他认为，我们所谓的"精神疾病"与身体疾病有着重要的区别。这是因为，他写道，"衡量精神疾病偏离的'规范'是一种心理社会和伦理的规范"。 8 也就是说，精神病学家认为某人是否疯狂，本质上取决于他们的主观判断，而不是客观的生物学测试。因此，从这个论点中，我们可以看到精神分析精神病学是建立在一个神话之上的——即精神疾病是真正的疾病这个神话——因为与身体医学中对正常状态的判断相比，精神分析对疾病的判断相对缺乏客观性。 9



THE POLITICS OF ANTI-PSYCHIATRY

反精神病学的政治



It should be noted that Szasz’s arguments – which he elaborated on in a range of books in the following decades – did not go unchallenged. His first book was incredibly controversial and brought swift retaliation from members of his own profession. For a start, he was quickly banned from teaching. And in turn his colleagues debated over whether he should be fired. When it came to his arguments, his more nuanced critics pointed out that his thinking rested on a range of untenable binaries between the body and mind, neurological and mental, problems in living and illness. This was not merely a theoretical issue either. Taking Szasz’s analysis seriously would mean excluding conditions widely seen as helpful to recognise. For instance, since the pathophysiology of migraines and cluster headaches is not well known, and their symptoms are ‘mental’, they would not count as genuine medical conditions worthy of support on Szasz’s framework.

值得注意的是，萨兹在其后数十年间通过一系列著作详述的观点并非未受质疑。他的首部著作引发了巨大争议，并迅速招致同行的猛烈反击。首先，他很快被禁止授课。随后，同事们就是否应解雇他展开辩论。针对其论点，较为审慎的批评者指出，他的思想建立在身心、神经与精神、生活困境与疾病之间一系列站不住脚的二元对立之上。这也不仅仅是理论问题。若认真采纳萨兹的分析框架，将意味着排除许多被广泛认为有必要识别的病症。例如，由于偏头痛和丛集性头痛的病理生理机制尚未明确，且其症状属于"精神"范畴，按照萨兹的标准，这些都不应被视为值得支持的真正医学病症。



For that matter, many patients did (and still do) find it helpful to see their psychological problems as mental illness or disability. Many also found state and professional support useful – yet all this would be undermined if Szasz’s views became widely accepted. Importantly, critique here came not just from patients but also came from other anti-psychiatrists. The Italian anti-fascist Franco Basaglia and his co-workers, who developed a dialectical materialist analysis to liberate inmates from the Trieste asylums and build a more humane mental health support system, rejected Szasz’s position. For them, the denial of mental illness was obviously absurd. Unlike Szasz, the Basaglians worked with patients who had experienced extreme mental health problems, and who saw this as illness rather than mere ordinary distress. Similarly, the equally radical Socialist Patients Collective, active in West Germany in the 1970s, held that mental illness was an undeniable fact, albeit primarily caused by capitalist domination and oppression.

就此而言，许多患者确实（并且至今仍然）认为将自己的心理问题视为精神疾病或残障是有帮助的。许多人还发现国家和专业支持是有用的——然而，如果萨斯（Szasz）的观点被广泛接受，所有这些都将受到破坏。重要的是，这里的批评不仅来自患者，也来自其他反精神病学人士。意大利反法西斯主义者弗朗哥·巴萨利亚（Franco Basaglia）及其同事，他们发展了一种辩证唯物主义的分析，以解放的里雅斯特精神病院的住院者，并建立一个更人性化的心理健康支持系统，他们拒绝了萨斯的立场。对他们来说，否认精神疾病显然是荒谬的。与萨斯不同，巴萨利亚派与那些经历过极端心理健康问题的患者合作，这些患者将此视为疾病，而不仅仅是普通的痛苦。同样，同样激进的社会主义患者集体（Socialist Patients Collective），在 1970 年代活跃于西德，认为精神疾病是一个不可否认的事实，尽管其主要原因在于资本主义的统治和压迫。



Despite the warnings of his Marxist critics, who saw Szasz’s views as a highly reactionary denial of mental illness, Szasz’s arguments quickly became influential. This was the case on the libertarian right, where Szasz himself sat, but also across the political spectrum. Anti-psychiatrists on the centre-left, such as Ronald Laing, and on the far-left, such as the communist David Cooper, sympathised with many aspects of Szasz’s arguments and developed their own analyses of madness, often in dialogue with Szasz’s work. Indeed, it was Cooper who coined the term ‘anti-psychiatry’ in 1967, which he used to group together Szasz with Laing and other rebel psychiatrists of the age.10 While the broader anti-psychiatry movement had a diversity of views, Szasz’s engaging writing, precise arguments, and powerful rhetoric helped his analysis become the dominant counter-narrative.

尽管他的马克思主义批评者警告说，萨兹的观点是对精神疾病的一种高度反动的否认，但他的论点迅速产生了影响力。这不仅在萨兹本人所属的自由意志主义右翼中如此，在整个政治光谱中也是如此。中左翼的反精神病学家，如罗纳德·莱恩，以及极左翼的，如共产主义者大卫·库珀，都对萨兹论点的许多方面表示同情，并发展了他们自己对疯狂的分析，这些分析常常与萨兹的著作进行对话。事实上，正是库珀在 1967 年创造了“反精神病学”一词，他用这个词将萨兹、莱恩以及那个时代的其他反叛精神病学家归为一类。 10 尽管更广泛的反精神病学运动观点多样，但萨兹引人入胜的写作、精确的论证和有力的修辞，帮助他的分析成为了主导性的反叙事。



Especially in the late 1960s as many counter-cultural and civil rights movements sprung up across the United States and beyond, anti-psychiatry was widely embraced alongside movements focusing on feminism, gay rights, and Black civil rights. The renowned 1976 Dialectics of Liberation conference in London, for instance, brought together anti-psychiatrists such as Laing and Cooper with the New Left intellectual Herbert Marcuse, the pan-Africanist Stokely Carmichael, and many other leading radical thinkers of the age.11 In turn, anti-psychiatry rhetoric and ideas were central to many of the uprisings and protests of 1968. By the early 1970s, as Michael Staub has written, ‘it would no longer be required to acknowledge Szasz’s name in connection with his ideas, so “universal” and accepted had they by this time become’.12 This was to the extent of helping bring about what Staub describes as a ‘revolution’13 not just in cultural understanding but also in legal approaches relating to mental illness, not least since it followed from Szasz’s arguments that the insanity defence was invalid.

尤其是在 20 世纪 60 年代末期，随着众多反主流文化和民权运动在美国乃至全球范围内兴起，反精神病学运动与聚焦女权、同性恋权利及黑人公民权利的运动一同获得了广泛接纳。例如，1976 年在伦敦举行的著名"解放辩证法"会议，就将莱恩和库珀等反精神病学家与新左派知识分子赫伯特·马尔库塞、泛非主义者斯托克利·卡迈克尔以及当时许多其他重要的激进思想家汇聚一堂。 11 相应地，反精神病学的言论和思想也成为 1968 年诸多起义和抗议活动的核心。正如迈克尔·斯托布所写，到 20 世纪 70 年代初，"提及这些观点时已不再需要提及萨斯的名字，因为它们此时已变得如此'普遍'和被接受"。 12 其影响之深远，甚至帮助促成了斯托布所描述的"革命" 13 ，这不仅体现在文化理解上，也体现在与精神疾病相关的法律途径中，尤其是它基于萨斯的论点，认为精神错乱辩护是无效的。



We see this in popular fictional accounts that adopted and further popularised Szaszian themes. The 1975 film adaption of Ken Kesey’s 1962 novel One Flew Over the Cuckoo’s Nest was especially popular, to the point of winning all five major Academy Awards. Starring Jack Nicholson as the protagonist Randle McMurphy, the film opens with McMurphy being put in a mental hospital after pretending to be insane to avoid prison. He ends up in a ward full of friendly inmates dominated and intimidated by cold and calculating staff. After being abused and controlled, McMurphy organises resistance and a plan to liberate the patients. Yet upon being caught, he is lobotomised – a far worse fate than would likely have awaited him in prison. Here we see all the core aspects of Szasz’s analysis: mental illness as an illusion, psychiatrists as unable to distinguish between genuine and false illness, and psychiatry as a form of social control masquerading as care.

这一点在流行虚构作品中尤为明显，它们采纳并进一步普及了萨斯式的主题。1975 年根据肯·凯西 1962 年小说改编的电影《飞越疯人院》尤其受欢迎，甚至包揽了奥斯卡五大主要奖项。影片由杰克·尼科尔森饰演主角兰德尔·麦克墨菲，故事以麦克墨菲为逃避监狱而假装精神失常被送入精神病院开场。他最终来到一个由冷漠精明的医护人员主导并恐吓、住满友善病患的病房。在遭受虐待和控制后，麦克墨菲组织起反抗并策划解放病友。然而在被发现后，他被迫接受了脑叶白质切除术——这远比他在监狱可能面临的命运更为悲惨。在此我们看到了萨斯分析的所有核心要素：精神疾病是一种幻象，精神病学家无法区分真假疾病，而精神病学则是伪装成关怀的社会控制形式。



It is important to stress that a key reason the Szaszian vision was able to become so influential was that most of the problems identified regarding the treatment of patients were all too real. The treatment of asylum inmates, for instance, was especially bad. Judi Chamberlin, an influential survivor activist, described one hospital as a ‘prison’ where there ‘was no phone, visitors were allowed only twice a week, and the locked ward door opened with a buzzer’.14 In many institutions patients were routinely denied basic human rights, tied up, and subjected to barbarous treatments such as lobotomy, whereby part of the brain was removed to make patients more docile. At the same time, psychiatrists regularly pathologised women as hysterical, Black civil rights protestors as psychotic, and queer people as inherently ill, in ways that reinforced and obscured deeply entrenched forms of social domination.

必须强调的是，萨兹式观点之所以能产生如此深远的影响，一个重要原因在于其所指出的患者治疗问题大多确凿存在。例如，精神病院收容者的待遇尤其恶劣。颇具影响力的幸存者活动家朱迪·钱伯林曾将某家医院描述为"监狱"，那里"没有电话，每周仅允许探视两次，上锁的病房门需通过蜂鸣器开启"。在许多机构中，患者的基本人权被系统性地剥夺，他们常被束缚，并遭受脑叶切除术等野蛮治疗——这种通过切除部分大脑使患者变得温顺的手段。与此同时，精神病学家惯于将女性病理化为"歇斯底里"，将黑人民权抗议者诊断为"精神错乱"，将酷儿群体定义为先天病态，这些做法既强化又掩盖了根深蒂固的社会支配形态。



Thus, a great many activists and members of the public alike were – rightly – increasingly concerned with what they saw as psychiatric overreach that functioned as a form of social control, and which justified human rights abuses and oppressive systems. And Freudians, having expanded the boundaries of pathology as well as having taken over the running of the asylums, took much of the blame for this. In turn, regardless of its errors and oversimplifications, the analysis of anti-psychiatry proponents, aided by popular fictional portrayals, was widely taken to help make sense of understandable worries about psychiatry.

因此，许多活动人士和公众都——理所当然地——越来越关注他们所认为的精神病学越界行为，这种行为作为一种社会控制形式，为侵犯人权和压迫性制度提供了正当理由。而弗洛伊德学派，由于扩大了病理学的边界并接管了精神病院的运营，为此承担了大部分责任。反过来，尽管存在错误和过度简化，反精神病学支持者的分析，在流行虚构作品的帮助下，被广泛认为有助于理解对精神病学的合理担忧。



The outcome of this was that for many then – and still today – it came to seem that the core problem for the mad and disabled was not just psychiatry itself but also the very concept of ‘mental illness’, not to mention psychiatric diagnoses, upon which its power was taken to be grounded. And the practical implication of this, for Szasz and his followers, would be that all manifestations of mental illness should be recast as non-medical ‘problems in living’. By invalidating ‘mental illness’ as a category for making sense of human suffering, the Szaszian project sought to undermine the conceptual root of psychiatric legitimacy. For they saw the social control of patients not as stemming from capital and the state, but rather from the very idea of mental illness itself.

其结果是，对于当时乃至今天的许多人来说，疯癫者和残疾人的核心问题似乎不仅仅是精神病学本身，还包括"精神疾病"这一基本概念，更不用说那些被视为精神病学权力基础的诊断了。对于萨兹及其追随者而言，这一观点的实际含义是，所有精神疾病的表现都应被重新定义为非医学性的"生活问题"。通过否定"精神疾病"作为理解人类苦难的范畴，萨兹式的方案试图从根本上动摇精神病学合法性的概念根基。因为他们认为，对患者的社会控制并非源于资本或国家，而是源于"精神疾病"这一观念本身。



THE CLOSING OF THE ASYLUMS

收容所的关闭



The effects of the support for anti-psychiatry were significant. We will come back to how it impacted our understandings of mental disorder later. For now, perhaps most importantly, by changing public perception, anti-psychiatry helped rapidly speed up a major shift that started in the 1950s: the closing of the asylums. While many inmates and their supporters had campaigned to close or reform the asylums since the nineteenth century, the anti-psychiatry proponents had more developed arguments that managed to change public perception significantly. In line with this tradition, for the more right-wing libertarian anti-psychiatrists such as Szasz in the United States and, albeit with a quite different analysis, the anti-fascist Franco Basaglia in Italy, the idea was that this would liberate these patients from the kinds of coercion and social control the mad and disabled had been subjected to since at least the eighteenth century. Hence as Andrew Scull writes, a ‘curious political alliance supported the dissolution of the state hospitals. On the left, a fierce opposition to the incarceration of the mentally ill in places that resembled prisons or warehouses for the unwanted’. But then on ‘the right, a libertarianism that hated the public provision of services of any sort, coupled with the promise of fiscal savings, made closure of state hospitals equally irresistible’.15

反精神病学运动所获得的支持产生了深远影响。我们稍后将探讨它如何重塑我们对精神障碍的理解。眼下最重要的是，通过改变公众认知，反精神病学运动极大地加速了始于 20 世纪 50 年代的重大转变：精神病院的关闭。尽管自 19 世纪以来，许多住院患者及其支持者就致力于关闭或改革精神病院，但反精神病学倡导者提出了更为系统的论点，成功显著改变了公众观念。秉承这一传统，对于更右翼的自由主义反精神病学家如美国的萨斯，以及持不同分析视角的意大利反法西斯主义者佛朗哥·巴萨利亚而言，其核心理念在于将患者从至少自 18 世纪以来精神病患和残障人士所遭受的强制措施与社会控制中解放出来。正如安德鲁·斯卡尔所写：“一个奇特的政治联盟支持解散国立医院。左翼阵营强烈反对将精神病患者囚禁在类似监狱或废弃仓库的场所。” 然而，在右翼阵营中，一种憎恶任何形式公共服务供给的自由主义思潮，加上削减财政开支的承诺，使得关闭公立医院同样变得势不可挡。 15



By the same token, the combination of popular books and acclaimed media portrayals brought simultaneous significant and widespread sympathy for the shift from asylum to ‘community’ care. The basic idea was that former inmates would return to their communities, and be supported to live at least relatively ordinary lives, free from coercion or control. Policies towards this shift began to be developed and implemented. By the end of the 1970s almost all the asylums had closed, with many old buildings sold off or left empty. In turn, many former inmates – some who had spent most of their lives inside the asylum walls – were released back into the communities from which they had originally come. Finally, it seemed to many proponents of the Szaszian approach, liberation was imminent.

同样地，畅销书籍与广受赞誉的媒体描绘相结合，为从收容所转向"社区"照护的变革赢得了广泛而深切的同情。其核心理念是让曾经的住院者回归社区，在免受强制或管控的前提下，获得支持以过上至少相对正常的生活。推动这一转变的政策开始制定并实施。到 1970 年代末，几乎所有收容所都已关闭，许多旧建筑被出售或闲置。相应地，大量曾经的住院者——其中有些人在收容所围墙内度过了大半生——被释放回他们最初来自的社区。在萨斯式疗法的众多支持者看来，解放终于近在眼前。



And yet despite the great hopes of the anti-psychiatrists, it increasingly became clear that their influence had not brought anything like widespread liberation. It is true that some former asylum inmates did manage to successfully return to their communities. And in a select few areas, some clinicians developed workable alternatives, and the shift to community care went well. Most notably, in the city of Trieste in Italy, Basaglia and his co-workers did manage to develop an effective alternative for patients in the community.16 Their system had no locked doors, and patients were closely supported by dedicated and caring staff.

然而，尽管反精神病学运动抱有巨大期望，但越来越明显的是，他们的影响并未带来广泛的解放。诚然，一些前精神病院患者确实成功回归了社区。在少数特定地区，一些临床医生开发了可行的替代方案，向社区护理的转型也进展顺利。最引人注目的是，在意大利的里雅斯特市，巴萨利亚及其同事确实为社区患者开发了一种有效的替代方案。 16 他们的系统没有上锁的门，患者得到了专注且富有爱心的员工的密切支持。



But in most cases, including across much of Europe and the United States, the closing of the asylums often did little to help former inmates. As Peter Sedgwick chronicled from England in 1982:

但在大多数情况下，包括欧洲大部分地区和美国，精神病院的关闭往往对前患者帮助甚微。正如彼得·塞奇威克在 1982 年从英国记录的那样：





In Britain no less than in the United States, ‘community care’ and ‘the replacement of the mental hospital’ were slogans which masked the growing depletion of real services for mental patients: the accumulating numbers of impaired, retarded and demented males in the prisons and common lodging-houses; the scarcity not only of local authority residential provision for the mentally disabled but of day centres and skilled social-work resources; the jettisoning of mental patients in their thousands into the isolated, helpless environment of their families of origin, who appealed in vain for hospital admission (even for a temporary period of respite), for counselling or support, and even for basic information and advice.17

在英国，与在美国一样，“社区护理”和“替代精神病院”这些口号掩盖了精神病患者实际服务日益减少的现实：监狱和普通寄宿所中受损、智力低下和痴呆的男性人数不断增加；不仅地方当局为精神残疾者提供的住宿设施稀缺，日间中心和专业社会工作资源也严重不足；成千上万的精神病患者被抛弃在孤立无援的原生家庭环境中，这些家庭徒劳地呼吁医院接收（即使只是暂时的喘息期）、寻求咨询或支持，甚至寻求基本的信息和建议。





Many former inmates struggled to find work, began using illegal drugs or entered criminalised professions and ended up in prison after breaking the law, much as Szasz had indicated was preferable. Indeed, as recent research by the historian Anne Parsons18 has shown, following the asylum closures, the prison industrial complex began to grow massively. But now it mainly incarcerated not just the (often) white former inmates of asylums. Rather, it grew to incarcerate, in much greater numbers, mad or disabled Black people alongside mad or disabled white people.

正如萨斯所暗示的那样，许多前收容所患者难以找到工作，开始使用非法药物或从事犯罪职业，最终因触犯法律而入狱。事实上，正如历史学家安妮·帕森斯 18 最近的研究所示，随着收容所的关闭，监狱工业综合体开始大规模扩张。但如今，它主要关押的已不仅仅是（通常是）白人前收容所患者。相反，其规模已扩大到关押数量远为庞大的黑人精神病患者或残障人士，以及白人精神病患者或残障人士。



Just as many younger inmates were shifted to prisons, many older inmates were shifted to the nursing home, where they were no freer than before. As Andrew Scull has chronicled:

正如许多年轻患者被转移到监狱一样，许多年长患者被转移到了养老院，在那里他们并未比以往更自由。正如安德鲁·斯卡尔所记载的那样：





Between 1963 and 1969 alone, the numbers of elderly patients with mental disorders living in nursing homes increased by nearly 200,000, from 187,675 to 367,586. By 1972, with some younger patients added to the mix, the mentally disturbed population housed in nursing and board-and-care homes had risen to 640,000, and two years later, it rose to 899,500.19

仅在 1963 年至 1969 年间，居住在养老院的精神障碍老年患者数量增加了近 20 万，从 187,675 人增至 367,586 人。到 1972 年，加上一些年轻患者，居住在养老院和寄宿护理之家的精神障碍人口已增至 64 万，两年后，这一数字上升至 899,500 人。 19





These nursing homes were carceral systems no less than the prisons or asylums were. Similar abuses as happened in the asylums also happened in the nursing homes, and sometimes the latter were even worse. Indeed, even when there is no abuse, recent research suggests that in nursing homes, newly admitted patients tend to both be younger and more likely to become long-term residents if they also have a mental illness.20 In retrospect it thus becomes apparent that rather than liberating patients from social control, anti-psychiatry helped facilitate their shift from one kind of carceral system to others that were often no better than the asylums.

这些养老院与监狱或精神病院无异，同样是监禁体系。精神病院中发生的类似虐待行为在养老院中同样存在，有时后者的情况甚至更为恶劣。事实上，即便没有虐待行为，近期研究表明，在养老院中，新入住的病人如果同时患有精神疾病，往往更年轻，也更可能成为长期居住者。 20 回顾过去，我们可以清楚地看到，反精神病学非但没有将病人从社会控制中解放出来，反而助长了他们从一种监禁体系转移到另一种往往不比精神病院好多少的体系中。



Indeed, as Scull21 has further detailed, support for anti-psychiatry even turned out to be useful for many states that wanted to save money. Due to gains in human rights and welfare support, fiscal pressures on the state intensified from the 1960s, leading to the remaining asylums being seen by governments as an overly costly waste of finances and resources. In the US, much of the change came down to specific states making manoeuvres to transfer costs on to federal government.22 Many older inmates were also moved to nursing homes for financial rather than clinical reasons, since this meant that states did not have to employ more staff at the asylums. In this, the Szaszian ideology turned out to be useful for the ruling class rather than helping to resist the dominant system.

诚如斯卡尔 21 进一步详述，反精神病学运动甚至被许多希望节省开支的国家视为有利工具。自 20 世纪 60 年代起，由于人权保障与福利支持力度的提升，国家财政压力日益加剧，政府逐渐将留存的精神病院视作过度消耗财力与资源的负担。在美国，这一转变很大程度上源于各州采取策略将成本转移至联邦政府。 22 许多年长的住院患者也因经济考量（而非临床需求）被迁往养老院，这使得各州无需在精神病院增聘工作人员。在此过程中，萨兹式的意识形态最终为统治阶级所用，而非助力抵抗主流体制。



At the same time, as we shall see in the following chapters, the increased availability of basic welfare support alongside new psychotropic drugs also made it more economically viable to close the last asylums, regardless of whether the available community support or alternative institutions would be sufficient for survival. If anything, this was especially enticing for governments following 1973, during which one of capitalism’s routine crises brought a great economic recession and mass unemployment. Hence, it is true that as the counter-cultural movements of the late 1960s and 1970s arose, the critique from anti-psychiatry certainly turned public opinion against the asylums as well as the very concept of mental illness. But in significant part, the asylums were shut down one by one, alongside rhetoric about returning patients to the community, to cut costs. And Szaszian scepticism regarding the reality of mental illness turned out to be useful for justifying this.
